,	O

;	O

Texas	B-Province
'	O

EIA	O
is	O
a	O
viral	O
disease	O
that	O
attacks	O
horses	O
'	O
immune	O
systems	O
.	O

The	O
virus	O
is	O
transmitted	O
through	O
the	O
exchange	O
of	O
body	O
fluids	O
from	O
an	O
infected	O
to	O
an	O
uninfected	O
animal	O
,	O
often	O
by	O
blood-feeding	O
insects	O
such	O
as	O
horseflies	O
.	O

It	O
can	O
also	O
be	O
transmitted	O
through	O
the	O
use	O
of	O
blood-contaminated	O
instruments	O
or	O
needles	O
.	O

A	O
Coggins	O
test	O
screens	O
horses	O
'	O
blood	O
for	O
antibodies	O
indicative	O
of	O
the	O
presence	O
of	O
the	O
EIA	O
virus	O
.	O

Most	O
US	O
states	O
require	O
horses	O
to	O
have	O
proof	O
of	O
a	O
negative	O
Coggins	O
test	O
to	O
travel	O
across	O
state	O
lines	O
.	O

Once	O

animal	O
is	O
infected	O
with	O
EIA	O
,	O
it	O
is	O
infected	O
for	O
life	O
and	O
can	O
be	O
a	O

for	O
the	O
spread	O
of	O
disease	O
.	O

Not	O

of	O
disease	O
,	O
but	O

doing	O
so	O

condition	O
loss	O
,	O
muscle	O

,	O
poor	O

,	O
fever	O
,	O
depression	O
,	O
and	O
anemia	O
.	O

EIA	O
has	O
no	O

and	O
no	O

.	O

A	O

away	O
from	O
unaffected	O

)	O
for	O
the	O

of	O
its	O
life	O
.	O
